msg:During the last two days of Hangzhou, I stayed at the Shili Fangfei Hotel in Xixi Wetland. Checking in and out of the hotel requires a boat ride, which is very ceremonial and very secluded. The hotel's front desk is near the entrance of Xixi, and the guest rooms and restaurants are on the small islands inside Xixi Wetland. The whole hotel is like a small village, with a very good environment and very clean. It's just that looking at the staff in white clothes will be a bit out of the play, and the divine song "New Creation" seems to ring in my ears, hahaha
Thank you for upgrading to the lakeside suite, which is very spacious and has a small courtyard by the water. The room facilities are very good, with Hansgrohe bathroom, Dyson hair dryer, Xiaomi TV and kettle. After checking in, the butler will add the guest's WeChat to facilitate contact and call the boat. Although the boat trips are quite frequent, the hotel is equipped with a restaurant, a cafe and a tea room. The restaurant has a good reputation for the children's playground. The food is generally good, and the lotus root powder for breakfast is super delicious!

msg:I have been looking forward to Shili Fangfei for a long time. It is an unforgettable and wonderful and unique stay experience! After registering at the front desk, take a boat ride along the stream. The grass on both sides of the bank is delicious and lush, as if you have entered the Peach Blossom Spring written by Tao Yuanming. It takes about 15 minutes by boat to reach Lihuawu where you are staying. The room is on the first floor of a small courtyard, with an entrance hall. The room layout is simple and warm, and there is a backyard garden. The bathroom is divided into three functional areas. It is awesome and makes you feel like you are at home. The best thing is the rich village-themed activities. I had a wonderful experience of Song Yun tea ordering with my children; at night, I strolled along the tree-lined avenue, walked across the small stone bridge, and watched an outdoor movie with a flashlight amidst the chirping of insects and the singing of cicadas in the countryside. Time passed by all at once. Back to my distant childhood. Shili Fangfei gave us more than just a stay-in experience. It was a wonderful trip and our children said they would come again!

This time I saw the paradise in real life! The Shili Fangfei Theme Resort in Xixi is simply the slow life I yearn for~
-

There are many activities in the village. You can have afternoon tea and play here. It is quite happy. You can also go there.
